vidhiḥ vidhānaṃ rasāyanābhidhānam ityarthaḥ  agre iti anantaram  vājīkaraṇaṃ cāgre abhidhāsyate iti śeṣaḥ  abheṣajamiti jñeyaṃ viparītaṃ yadauṣadhāt tadasevyaṃ niṣevyaṃ tu pravakṣyāmi yadauṣadham  Caryurvedadīpikāabheṣajamapi pūrvoddiṣṭaṃ vivṛṇotyabheṣajamityādi  viparītaṃ rogajananalakṣaṇārthakāri  rasāyanānāṃ dvividhaṃ prayogamṛṣayo viduḥ kuṭīprāveśikaṃ caiva vātātapikameva ca sa prayogaḥ ayaṃ tu rasāyanaviṣayaḥ   bhallātakānāṃ jarjarīkṛtānāṃ piṣṭasvedanaṃ pūrayitvā bhūmāv ākaṇṭhaṃ nikhātasya snehabhāvitasyadṛḍhasyopari kumbhasyāropyoḍupenāpidhāya kṛṣṇamṛttikāvaliptaṃ gomayāgnibhir upasvedayetteṣāṃ yaḥ svarasaḥ kumbhaṃ prapadyeta tam aṣṭabhāgamadhusamprayuktaṃ dviguṇaghṛtamadyāt tatprayogādvarṣaśatamajaraṃ vayastiṣṭhatīti samānaṃ pūrveṇa  Caryurvedadīpikā guḍabhallātakaṃ bhallātakayūṣaḥbhallātakatailaṃ bhallātakapalalaṃ bhallātakasaktavaḥ bhallātakalavaṇaṃ bhallātakatarpaṇamiti bhallātakavidhānamuktaṃ bhavati  Caryurvedadīpikābhallātakasarpir ityādayo daśaprayogāḥ  atra ca yathāyogyatayā bhallātakena sarpirādīnāṃ saṃskāraḥ saṃyogaśca jñeyaḥ  yaduktaṃ jatūkarṇe bhallātakasaṃyuktasaṃskṛtāni ca ghṛtakṣīrakṣaudraguḍayūṣatailapalalasaktulavaṇatarpaṇāni bhallātakam antardhūmadagdhaṃ grāhyam  anye tu sarpirādīnāṃ sarveṣāmeva bhallātakena saṃskāraṃ vyākhyānayanti  iha saktuprayogodravottaratvād aviśeṣakarmaṇā bhedanīyaḥ  bhallātakāni tīkṣṇāni Carprayogaḥ saptasaptāhās trayaś caikaśca saptakaḥ nirdiṣṭas trividhastasya paro madhyovarastathā  Carpalamardhapalaṃ karṣo mātrā tasya tridhā matā yurvedadīpikāśilājatubhāvanāvidhim āha Caryurvedadīpikāsaṃśrutyeti pratijñāya  cikitsaiva paṇyaṃ vikretavyamiti cikitsāpaṇyam  te hitvetyādau dharmārthaṃ kriyamāṇacikitsā mahāphalatvena kāñcanarāśitulyā itarā tv asārakalpā pāṃśurāśitulyā  vaivasvatakṣayamiti yamagṛham  āyurvedasamutthānaṃ divyauṣadhividhiṃ śubham amṛtālpāntaraguṇaṃ siddhaṃ ratnarasāyanam  Carsiddhebhyo brahmacāribhyo yaduvācāmareśvaraḥ āyurvedasamutthāne tat sarvaṃ saṃprakāśitam  Carityagniveśakṛte tantre carakapratisaṃskṛte cikitsitasthāne rasāyanādhyāye āyurvedasamutthānīyo nāma rasāyanapādaścaturthaḥ  Caryurvedadīpikāsaṃgrahe ratnarasāyanamiti hemādiratnasaṃyuktaṃ rasāyanam   āyurvedasamutthāne prakāśitatayā divyauṣadhividhyādi yaduvāca brahmacāribhyomareśvaraḥ tat saṃprakāśitam iti yojanā    CarakasaṃhitāCikitsāsthāna Vājīkaraṇādhyāya Saṃyogaśaramūlīyaathātaḥ saṃyogaśaramūlīyaṃ vājīkaraṇapādaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ  Cariti ha smāha bhagavānātreyaḥ  Caryurvedadīpikā svasthorjaskaratvasāmānyāt rasāyanamanu vājīkaraṇaṃ vācyaṃ tatrāpi vājīkaraṇe pravṛttyupadarśakaprakaraṇayuktatvād ādau saṃyogaśaramūlīya ucyate saṃyogaḥ śaramūlānām asminn astīti saṃyogaśaramūlīyaḥ  vājīkaraṇam anvicchet puruṣo nityamātmavān tadāyattau hi dharmārthau prītiśca yaśa eva ca  Carputrasyāyatanaṃ hy etadguṇāścaite sutāśrayāḥ yurvedadīpikāavājī vājīvātyarthaṃ maithune śaktaḥ kriyate yena tad vājīkaraṇam  uktaṃ hi vājīvātibalo yena yātyapratihataḥ striyam ityādi  anvicchediti rasāyanānmahāphalāt tadapekṣayālpaphalaṃ vājīkaraṇaṃ paścād icchet  puruṣa iti padena taruṇapuruṣagrāhiṇā bālavṛddhau niṣiddhavyavāyau nirākaroti  uktaṃ hi atibālo hy asaṃpūrṇasarvadhātuḥ striyo vrajan upatapyeta sahasā taḍāgamiva kājalam  śuṣkaṃ rūkṣaṃ yathā kāṣṭhaṃ jantujagdhaṃ vijarjaram spṛṣṭamāśu viśīryeta tathā vṛddhaḥ striyo vrajan iti  nityamityanena na rasāyanavat saṃprayogo vṛṣyasya kiṃtv āhāravat sarvadoṣayoga iti darśayati  ātmavānityanena durātmano vṛṣyakaraṇaṃ niṣedhati sa hi vṛṣyopayogādupacitadhātuḥ sann agamyāgamanamapi kuryāt  dharmādayo vṛṣyāyattā eva yathā bhavanti tadāha putrasyetyādi  āyatanaṃ kāraṇam  ete guṇā iti dharmādayaḥ vṛṣyaprayogajanitaḥ putro dharmādīn pituḥ sampādayatītyarthaḥ  vājīkaraṇasevayā ceha yuktayaiva ṛtukāle ca maithunaṃ prādhānyenābhipretaṃ tena tisraiṣaṇīyetraya upastambhāḥ ityādigranthena brahmacaryaṃ yaduktaṃ tad ṛtukāle yathāvidhikṛtamaithunāpratiṣedhakamiti na virodhaḥ  vājīkaraṇam agryaṃ ca kṣetraṃ strī yā praharṣiṇī  Cariṣṭā hy ekaikaśo py arthāḥ paraṃ prītikarāḥ smṛtāḥ kiṃ punaḥ strīśarīre ye saṃghātena pratiṣṭhitāḥ  Carsaṃghāto hīndriyārthānāṃ strīṣu nānyatra vidyate stryāśrayo hīndriyārtho yaḥ sa prītijananodhikam strīṣu prītirviśeṣeṇa strīṣv apatyaṃ pratiṣṭhitam  Cardharmārthau strīṣu lakṣmīśca strīṣu lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ surūpā yauvanasthā yā lakṣaṇairyā vibhūṣitā  Caryā vaśyā śikṣitā yā ca sā strī vṛṣyatamā matā yurvedadīpikāsarvavājīkaraṇebhyaḥ pradhānarūpaṃ vājīkaraṇamāha vājītyādi  kṣetramiva kṣetraṃ tatra śukrarūpabījaprarohaṇāt  arthā iti śabdādayaḥ te ca strīgatādhararasakalaviṅkarutarūpādayaḥ prasiddhā eva  dharmārthau strīṣviti sahaiva patnyā dharmaścarya ityādyupadeśād dharmaḥ tathānuraktā gṛhiṇī artharakṣaṇādi karotītyartha ityarthaḥ  striyā lakṣmyāḥ saṃyoge dhanasampad bhavatīti strīṣu lakṣmīḥ pratiṣṭhitetyarthaḥ  vaśyā āyattā  śikṣiteti kāmaśāstroktagītavāditralāsyādicatuḥṣaṣṭikalāśikṣitā  nānābhaktyā tu lokasya daivayogācca yoṣitām  Cartaṃ taṃ prāpya vivardhante naraṃ rūpādayo guṇāḥ vayorūpavacohāvair yā yasya paramāṅganā  Carpraviśatyāśu hṛdayaṃ daivād vā karmaṇo pi vā hṛdayotsavarūpā yā yā samānamanaḥśayā  Carsamānasattvā yā vaśyā yā yasya prīyate priyaiḥ yā pāśabhūtā sarveṣām indriyāṇāṃ parairguṇaiḥ  Caryayā viyukto nistrīkam aratir manyate jagat yasyā ṛte śarīraṃ nā dhatte śūnyam ivendriyaiḥ  Carśokodvegāratibhayair yāṃ dṛṣṭvā nābhibhūyate yāti yāṃ prāpya visrambhaṃ dṛṣṭvā hṛṣyatyatīva yām  Carapūrvāmiva yāṃ yāti nityaṃ harṣātivegataḥ gatvā gatvāpi bahuśo yāṃ tṛptiṃ naiva gacchati  Carsā strī vṛṣyatamā tasya nānābhāvā hi mānavāḥ atulyagotrāṃ vṛṣyāṃ ca prahṛṣṭāṃ nirupadravām  Carśuddhasnātāṃ vrajennārīmapatyārthī nirāmayaḥ yurvedadīpikārūpādivyatirekeṇāpi kācit kasyacit karmavaśādvṛṣyā strī bhavatīti darśayannāha nānetyādi  daivayogāditi prāktanakarmavaśāt  vivardhanta iti vṛṣyatvaṃ sampādayanti  hāvo naraṃ prati strīṇāṃ śṛṅgāraceṣṭāviśeṣaḥ  uktaṃ ca bharatena prakāśarūpakaṃ sattvaṃ sattvotplavāḥ samudgatāḥ  tebhyo hāvādiniṣpattirityāhuḥ paramarṣayaḥ iti  daivād iti prāktanakarmaṇaḥ  karmaṇa iti aihikādvaśīkaraṇādikarmaṇaḥ  manaḥśayaḥ kāmaḥ  pāśabhūteti manaindriyabandhahetutvāt  nānābhāvā hi mānavāḥ ityanena rūpādiguṇayogena sarvapuruṣān prati strīṇāṃ priyatvamiti darśayati  acchāyaś caikaśākhaś ca niṣphalaśca yathā drumaḥ  Caraniṣṭagandhaścaikaśca nirapatyastathā naraḥ citradīpaḥ saraḥ śuṣkam adhātur dhātusaṃnibhaḥ  Carniṣprajas tṛṇapūlīti mantavyaḥ puruṣākṛtiḥ apratiṣṭhaśca nagnaśca śūnyaścaikendriyaśca nā  Carmantavyo niṣkriyaścaiva yasyāpatyaṃ na vidyate bahumūrtir bahumukho bahuvyūho bahukriyaḥ  Carbahucakṣur bahujñāno bahvātmā ca bahuprajaḥ maṅgalyoyaṃ praśasyoyaṃ dhanyoyaṃ vīryavān ayam  Carbahuśākhoyamiti ca stūyate nā bahuprajaḥ prītirbalaṃ sukhaṃ vṛttir vistāro vipulaṃ kulam  Caryaśo lokāḥ sukhodarkāstuṣṭiś cāpatyasaṃśritāḥ tasmādapatyamanvicchan guṇāṃścāpatyasaṃśritān  Carvājīkaraṇanityaḥ syādicchan kāmasukhāni ca upabhogasukhān siddhān vīryāpatyavivardhanān  Carvājīkaraṇasaṃyogān pravakṣyāmyata uttaram yurvedadīpikāsamprati vṛṣyaprayogasādhyasya putrasyopādeyetāṃ darśayannāha acchāya ityādi  ekaśākha iti ekasvarūpa ityarthaḥ  citralikhito dīpaścitradīpaḥ  adhātur dhātusaṃnibha iti asuvarṇādirūpaḥ suvarṇādivad ābhāsate yo jātuṣakaṅkaṇādiḥ  pūlī napuṃsakadharmitvāt  tṛṇapūlī puruṣākṛtiriti bhāṣayā puruṣārthakriyāvirahitvaṃ darśayati  kāmasukhāni cetyanena putrotpādātiriktaṃ nātiślāghyaṃ phalaṃ darśayati  kāmasukhāni hi aihikānyeva paraṃ na putravad ubhayalokopakārakāṇi  upabhoge maithune sukhaṃ kurvantītyupabhogasukhāḥ kiṃvā upabhoktuṃ sukhā upabhogasukhāḥ vīryaṃ śukram  śaramūlekṣumūlāni kāṇḍekṣuḥ sekṣubālikā  Carśatāvarī payasyā ca vidārī kaṇṭakārikā jīvantī jīvako medā vīrā carṣabhako balā  Carṛddhir gokṣurakaṃ rāsnā sātmaguptā punarnavā eṣāṃ tripalikān bhāgān māṣāṇām āḍhakaṃ navam  Carvipācayejjaladroṇe caturbhāgaṃ ca śeṣayet tatra peṣyāṇi madhukaṃ drākṣā phalgūni pippalī  Carātmaguptā madhūkāni kharjūrāṇi śatāvarī vidāryāmalakekṣūṇāṃ rasasya ca pṛthak pṛthak  Carsarpiṣaś cāḍhakaṃ dadyāt kṣīradroṇaṃ ca tadbhiṣak sādhayedghṛtaśeṣaṃ ca supūtaṃ yojayet punaḥ  Carśarkarāyāstugākṣīryāś cūrṇaiḥ prasthonmitaiḥ pṛthak palaiś caturbhir māgadhyāḥ palena maricasya ca  Cartvagelākesarāṇāṃ ca cūrṇair ardhapalonmitaiḥ madhunaḥ kuḍavābhyāṃ ca dvābhyāṃ tatkārayedbhiṣak  Carpalikā gulikāstyānāstā yathāgni prayojayet eṣa vṛṣyaḥ paraṃ yogo bṛṃhaṇo balavardhanaḥ  Caranenāśva ivodīrṇo balī liṅgaṃ samarpayet yurvedadīpikākāṇḍekṣuḥ bṛhadikṣuḥ  ikṣubālikā khaggālikā  payasyā kṣīravidārī  vīrā kṣīrakākolī  phalguḥ kāṣṭhodumbarikā  śatāvarītyantena kalkacchedaḥ  vaṃśarocanā tugākṣīrī anye vaṃśarocanānukāri pārthivadravyaṃ tāladhīti vadanti  styānā iti ghanāḥ  māṣāṇāmātmaguptāyā bījānāmāḍhakaṃ navam  Carjīvakarṣabhakau vīrāṃ medām ṛddhiṃ śatāvarīm madhukaṃ cāśvagandhāṃ ca sādhayet kuḍavonmitām  Carrase tasmin ghṛtaprasthaṃ gavyaṃ daśaguṇaṃ payaḥ vidārīṇāṃ rasaprasthaṃ prasthamikṣurasasya ca  Cardattvā mṛdvagninā sādhyaṃ siddhaṃ sarpirnidhāpayet śarkarāyāstugākṣīryāḥ kṣaudrasya ca pṛthak pṛthak  Carbhāgāṃścatuṣpalāṃs tatra pippalyāścāvapet palam palaṃ pūrvamato līḍhvā tatonnam upayojayet  Carya icchedakṣayaṃ śukraṃ śephasaś cottamaṃ balam yurvedadīpikādvitīyaprayoge rase iti kvāthe  śarkarā māṣavidalāstugākṣīrī payo ghṛtam  Cargodhūmacūrṇaṣaṣṭhāni sarpiṣy utkārikāṃ pacet tāṃ nātipakvāṃ mṛditāṃ kaukkuṭe madhure rase  Carsugandhe prakṣiped uṣṇe yathā sāndrībhaved rasaḥ eṣa piṇḍaraso vṛṣyaḥ pauṣṭiko balavardhanaḥ  Caranenāśva ivodīrṇo balī liṅgaṃ samarpayet śikhitittirihaṃsānāmevaṃ piṇḍaraso mataḥ balavarṇasvarakaraḥ pumāṃstena vṛṣāyate  Caryurvedadīpikāutkārikā mūṣikotkarākārā  śikhitittirihaṃsānāṃ piṇḍarasair vyastasamastāś catvāraḥ piṇḍarasāḥ  ghṛtaṃ māṣān sabastāṇḍān sādhayenmāhiṣe rase bharjayettaṃ rasaṃ pūtaṃ phalāmlaṃ navasarpiṣi  Carīṣat salavaṇaṃ yuktaṃ dhānyajīrakanāgaraiḥ eṣa vṛṣyaśca balyaśca bṛṃhaṇaśca rasottamaḥ  Carcaṭakāṃstittirirase tittirīn kaukkuṭe rase kukkuṭān bārhiṇarase hāṃse bārhiṇameva ca  Carnavasarpiṣi saṃtaptān phalāmlān kārayed rasān madhurānvā yathāsātmyaṃ gandhāḍhyān balavardhanān  Cartṛptiṃ caṭakamāṃsānāṃ gatvā yo nupibet payaḥ na tasya liṅgaśaithilyaṃ syānna śukrakṣayo niśi  Carmāṣasūpeṇa yo bhuktvā ghṛtāḍhyaṃ ṣaṣṭikaudanam payaḥ pibati rātriṃ sa kṛtsnāṃ jāgarti vegavān na nā svapiti rātriṣu nityastabdhena śephasā tṛptaḥ kukkuṭamāṃsānāṃ bhṛṣṭānāṃ nakraretasi  Carniḥsrāvya matsyāṇḍarasaṃ bhṛṣṭaṃ sarpiṣi bhakṣayet  Carhaṃsabarhiṇadakṣāṇām evamaṇḍāni bhakṣayet  Caryurvedadīpikāniśītyanena sakalaniśāmaithune pīti darśayati  haṃsetyādi haṃsabarhidakṣāṇām aṇḍaprayogā yadyapi bhinnāḥ tathāpi prayogāpekṣayā eka evāyaṃ prayogaḥ  evaṃ saṃgrahoktāḥ haṃsabarhidakṣāṇām ekaprayogeṇa pañcadaśaprayogāḥ pūryante  srotaḥsu śuddheṣvamale śarīre vṛṣyaṃ yadā nā mitamatti kāle vṛṣāyate tena paraṃ manuṣyas tadbṛṃhaṇaṃ caiva balapradaṃ ca  Cartasmāt purā śodhanameva kāryaṃ balānurūpaṃ na hi vṛṣyayogāḥ sidhyanti dehe maline prayuktāḥ kliṣṭe yathā vāsasi rāgayogāḥ  Caryurvedadīpikāvṛṣyayogāśca śuddhadehaireva kartavyā iti darśayannāha srotaḥsvityādi  mitamiti mātrāvat  kliṣṭe iti mlāne  vājīkaraṇasāmarthyaṃ kṣetraṃ strī yasya caiva yā ye doṣā nirapatyānāṃ guṇāḥ putravatāṃ ca ye  Cardaśa pañca ca saṃyogā vīryāpatyavivardhanāḥ uktāste śaramūlīye pāde puṣṭibalapradāḥ  Carityagniveśakṛte tantre carakapratisaṃskṛte cikitsāsthāne vājīkaraṇādhyāye saṃyogaśaramūlīyo nāma vājīkaraṇapādaḥ prathamaḥ  Caryurvedadīpikāsaṃgrahe yasya caiva yeti yasya yā vṛṣyetyarthaḥ   CarakasaṃhitāCikitsāsthāna Vājīkaraṇādhyāya siktakṣīrikaathāta āsiktakṣīrikaṃ vājīkaraṇapādaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ  Cariti ha smāha bhagavānātreyaḥ  Caryurvedadīpikāāsiktakṣīrikaṃ vṛṣyapādābhidhānaprasaṅgāt padāntasya viśiṣṭasambandhāvayavatayocyate   āsiktakṣīramiti padam asty asminn iti āsiktakṣīrī tatra svārthikaḥ kapratyayaḥ kiṃvā ḍhakpratyayena vaiśeṣikaśabdavat āsiktakṣīrika iti sādhanīyam āsiktakṣīram āpūrṇam aśuṣkaṃ śuddhaṣaṣṭikam udūkhale samāpothya pīḍayet kṣīramarditam  Cargṛhītvā taṃ rasaṃ pūtaṃ gavyena payasā saha bījānāmātmaguptāyā dhānyamāṣarasena ca  Carbalāyāḥ śūrpaparṇyāśca jīvantyā jīvakasya ca ṛddhyarṣabhakakākolīśvadaṃṣṭrāmadhukasya ca  Carśatāvaryā vidāryāśca drākṣākharjūrayor api saṃyuktaṃ mātrayā vaidyaḥ sādhayettatra cāvapet  Cartugākṣīryāḥ samāṣāṇāṃ śālīnāṃ ṣaṣṭikasya ca godhūmānāṃ ca cūrṇāni yaiḥ sa sāndrībhavedrasaḥ  Carsāndrībhūtaṃ ca kuryāt prabhūtamadhuśarkaram guṭikā badaraistulyāstāś ca sarpiṣi bharjayet  Cartā yathāgni prayuñjānaḥ kṣīramāṃsarasāśanaḥ paśyatyapatyaṃ vipulaṃ vṛddho pyātmajamakṣayam  Caryurvedadīpikāāsiktakṣīramiti kṣīrasekavṛddham  yaduktaṃ jatūkarṇe kṣīrasekavṛddhaṃ ṣaṣṭikaṃ pakvam ityādi  śuddhaṣaṣṭikamiti gauraṣaṣṭikam  atra balādirasānāṃ tulyamānatāḥ kiṃvā mātrāśabdasyālpavacanatvād balādirasānām alpamātratvam  prakṣepyacūrṇapramāṇam āha yaiḥ sa sāndrībhaved rasa iti yāvanmānena cūrṇena rasasya sāndratā bhavati tāvanmātraṃ cūrṇaṃ grāhyam  prabhūtatvaṃ madhuśarkarayor yāvatātyarthamadhuratvaṃ syāt tāvajjñeyam   atra ca prayogamahimnaiva madhuyuktasyāpi prayogasya bharjanakriyāyām agnisaṃyogo na virodham āvahati tathā hi suśrute pi triphalāyaskṛtau  madhuno gnisambandho bhavatyeva   ātmajamiti harṣabhūtātmajaṃ śukramiti yāvat  caṭakānāṃ sahaṃsānāṃ dakṣāṇāṃ śikhināṃ tathā śiśumārasya nakrasya bhiṣakśukrāṇi saṃharet  Cargavyaṃ sarpir varāhasya kuliṅgasya vasāmapi ṣaṣṭikānāṃ ca cūrṇāni cūrṇaṃ godhūmakasya ca  Carebhiḥ pūpalikāḥ kāryāḥ śaṣkulyo vartikāstathā pūpā dhānāś ca vividhā bhakṣyāścānye pṛthagvidhāḥ  Careṣāṃ prayogādbhakṣyāṇāṃ stabdhenāpūrṇaretasā śephasā vājivadyāti yāvadicchaṃ striyo naraḥ  Carātmaguptāphalaṃ māṣān kharjūrāṇi śatāvarīm śṛṅgāṭakāni mṛdvīkāṃ sādhayetprasṛtonmitam  Carkṣīraprasthaṃ jalaprasthametat prasthāvaśeṣitam śuddhena vāsasā pūtaṃ yojayet prasṛtais tribhiḥ  Carśarkarāyāstugākṣīryāḥ sarpiṣo bhinavasya ca tat pāyayet sakṣaudraṃ ṣaṣṭikānnaṃ ca bhojayet  Carjarāparītopyabalo yogenānena vindati naropatyaṃ suvipulaṃ yuveva ca sa hṛṣyati  Caryurvedadīpikādakṣaḥ kukkuṭaḥ  śukrāṇīti yadyapyuktaṃ tathāpi caṭakādiśukragrahaṇasyāśakyatvāt samānaguṇāni tadaṇḍānyapīha gṛhyante  vartikā vartyākārā bhakṣyāḥ  dhānā iti dhānākārā bhakṣyāḥ  ayaṃ tulyadravyatayā vividhabhakṣyarūpo pyeka eva yogaḥ  kharjūrīmastakaṃ māṣān payasyāṃ ca śatāvarīm kharjūrāṇi madhūkāni mṛdvīkāmajaḍāphalam  Carpalonmitāni matimān sādhayet salilāḍhake tena pādāvaśeṣeṇa kṣīraprasthaṃ vipācayet  Carkṣīraśeṣeṇa tenādyād ghṛtāḍhyaṃ ṣaṣṭikaudanam saśarkareṇa saṃyoga eṣa vṛṣyaḥ paraṃ smṛtaḥ  Caryurvedadīpikāajaḍā śūkaśimbī  jīvakarṣabhakau medāṃ jīvantīṃ śrāvaṇīdvayam kharjūraṃ madhukaṃ drākṣāṃ pippalīṃ viśvabheṣajam  Carśṛṅgāṭakaṃ vidārīṃ ca navaṃ sarpiḥ payo jalam siddhaṃ ghṛtāvaśeṣaṃ taccharkarākṣaudrapādikam  Carṣaṣṭikānnena saṃyuktamupayojyaṃ yathābalam vṛṣyaṃ balyaṃ ca varṇyaṃ ca kaṇṭhyaṃ bṛṃhaṇam uttamam  Caryurvedadīpikājīvaketyādau vidāryantaiḥ kalkaiḥ kṣīrajalābhyāṃ ghṛtaṃ sādhanīyam  dadhnaḥ saraṃ śaraccandrasaṃnibhaṃ doṣavarjitam śarkarākṣaudramaricais tugākṣīryā ca buddhimān  Caryuktyā yuktaṃ sasūkṣmailaṃ nave kumbhe śucau paṭe mārjitaṃ prakṣipecchīte ghṛtāḍhye ṣaṣṭikaudane  Carpibenmātrāṃ rasālāyāstaṃ bhuktvā ṣaṣṭikaudanam varṇasvarabalopetaḥ pumāṃstena vṛṣāyate  Caryurvedadīpikāyuktyeti yathā kaṭutvādyadhikaṃ na bhavati tathā maricādiyogaḥ kartavyaḥ prayuñjāno vṛṣāyate  Cartapte sarpiṣi nakrāṇḍaṃ tāmracūḍāṇḍamiśritam yuktaṃ ṣaṣṭikacūrṇena sarpiṣābhinavena ca  Carpaktvā pūpalikāḥ khādedvāruṇīmaṇḍapo naraḥ ya icchedaśvavad gantuṃ prasektuṃ gajavac ca yaḥ  Caryurvedadīpikācandrāṃśukalpamiti atyarthaśuklam  etaiḥ prayogairvidhivadvapuṣmān vīryopapanno balavarṇayuktaḥ harṣānvito vājivad aṣṭavarṣo bhavet samarthaśca varāṅganāsu  Caryadyacca kiṃcin manasaḥ priyaṃ syādramyā vanāntāḥ pulināni śailāḥ iṣṭāḥ striyo bhūṣaṇagandhamālyaṃ priyā vayasyāśca tadatra yogyam  Caryurvedadīpikāatra yogyam iti vṛṣyaprayogasamartham  āsiktakṣīrike pāde ye yogāḥ parikīrtitāḥ aṣṭāv apatyakāmaiste prayojyāḥ pauruṣārthibhiḥ  Carityagniveśakṛte tantre carakapratisaṃskṛte cikitsāsthāne vājīkaraṇādhyāye āsiktakṣīriko nāma vājīkaraṇapādo dvitīyaḥ  Caryurvedadīpikāpauruṣārthibhiriti śukrārthibhiḥ   CarakasaṃhitāCikitsāsthāna Vājīkaraṇādhyāya Māṣaparṇabhṛtīyaathāto māṣaparṇabhṛtīyaṃ vājīkaraṇapādaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ  Cariti ha smāha bhagavānātreyaḥ  Caryurvedadīpikāmāṣaparṇabhṛtīyasambandho pi pūrvavat  māṣaparṇabhṛtāṃ dhenuṃ gṛṣṭiṃ puṣṭāṃ catuḥstanīm samānavarṇavatsāṃ ca jīvadvatsāṃ ca buddhimān  Carrohiṇīmathavā kṛṣṇām ūrdhvaśṛṅgīm adāruṇām ikṣvādām arjunādāṃ vā sāndrakṣīrāṃ ca dhārayet  Carkevalaṃ tu payastasyāḥ śṛtaṃ vāśṛtameva vā śarkarākṣaudrasarpirbhiryuktaṃ tadvṛṣyamuttamam  Caryurvedadīpikāgṛṣṭim ekavāraprasūtām  catuḥstanīm ityanena sampūrṇacatuḥstanīṃ darśayati  rohiṇīmiti lohitavarṇām  ūrdhvaśṛṅgatvaṃ viśuddhabahukṣīrāyā eva bhavatīti vacanājjñeyam  ikṣvādeti ikṣudaṇḍabhakṣā  arjunādā arjunavṛkṣapattrabhakṣā  ikṣvādā vā arjunādā vā māṣaparṇabhṛtā veti vikalpatrayam  payaḥ śṛtamaśṛtaṃ veti dvau yogau  śarkarākṣaudrasarpirbhiryuktaṃ taditi tṛtīyaḥ  etatprayogopi jatūkarṇe tasyāḥ kṣīraṃ śarkarākṣaudrayuktaṃ vā kevalaṃ śṛtamaśṛtaṃ veti  śukralair jīvanīyaiśca bṛṃhaṇair balavardhanaiḥ kṣīrasaṃjananaiścaiva payaḥ siddhaṃ pṛthak pṛthak  Caryuktaṃ godhūmacūrṇena saghṛtakṣaudraśarkaram paryāyeṇa prayoktavyamicchatā śukramakṣayam  Caryurvedadīpikāparyāyeṇeti pṛthak pṛthak prayoktavyaṃ tena pañcabhirgaṇaiḥ pañca yogā bhavanti  medāṃ payasyāṃ jīvantīṃ vidārīṃ kaṇṭakārikām śvadaṃṣṭrāṃ kṣīrikāṃ māṣān godhūmāñchāliṣaṣṭikān  Carpayasyardhodake paktvā kārṣikān āḍhakonmite vivarjayet payaḥśeṣaṃ tatpūtaṃ kṣaudrasarpiṣā  Caryuktaṃ saśarkaraṃ pītvā vṛddhaḥ saptatiko pi vā vipulaṃ labhatepatyaṃ yuveva ca sa hṛṣyati  Caryurvedadīpikāvivarjayed iti medādikalkaṃ varjayet  vṛddhaḥ saptaterarvāgiti jñeyam  saptatikasya tu yadyapi śukranivṛttiruktā tathāpi vṛṣyaprabhāvād bhavatīti vijñeyam  maṇḍalairjātarūpasya tasyā eva payaḥ śṛtam apatyajananaṃ siddhaṃ saghṛtakṣaudraśarkaram  Caryurvedadīpikājātarūpasyeti suvarṇasya maṇḍalarūpākṛtir iha suvarṇasya prabhāvādvṛṣyaprayogopakāriṇī bhavatīti vacanājjñeyam  tasyā eveti māṣaparṇabhṛtadhenvāḥ  triṃśat supiṣṭāḥ pippalyaḥ prakuñce tailasarpiṣoḥ bhṛṣṭāḥ saśarkarakṣaudrāḥ kṣīradhārāvadohitāḥ  Carpītvā yathābalaṃ cordhvaṃ ṣaṣṭikaṃ kṣīrasarpiṣā bhuktvā na rātrim astabdhaṃ liṅgaṃ paśyati nā kṣarat  Carśvadaṃṣṭrāyā vidāryāśca rase kṣīracaturguṇe ghṛtāḍhyaḥ sādhito vṛṣyo māṣaṣaṣṭikapāyasaḥ  Caryurvedadīpikāprakuñcaṃ palam  kṣīradhārāvadohitā iti pippalīkalkād upari kṣīradhārāvadohaḥ kartavyaḥ kṣīraṃ ca tāvaddohyaṃ yāvatā pānayogyāḥ pippalyo bhavanti  phalānāṃ jīvanīyānāṃ snigdhānāṃ rucikāriṇām kuḍavaścūrṇitānāṃ syāt svayaṃguptāphalasya ca  Carkuḍavaścaiva māṣāṇāṃ dvau dvau ca tilamudgayoḥ godhūmaśālicūrṇānāṃ kuḍavaḥ kuḍavo bhavet  Carsarpiṣaḥ kuḍavaścaikastat sarvaṃ kṣīramarditam paktvā pūpalikāḥ khāded bahvyaḥ syur yasya yoṣitaḥ  Caryurvedadīpikāphalānāmityādi  phalānāmiti jīvanīyānām ityādibhis tribhiḥ pratyekam abhisaṃbadhyate  jīvanīyānāmiti ṣaṭkakaṣāyavargoktānāṃ jīvakarṣabhādīnāṃ daśānām  snigdhānāmiti snehopagānāṃ mṛdvīkādīnāṃ daśānāṃ saptakakaṣāyavargoktānām  tathā rucikāriṇām iti catuṣkakaṣāyavargoktānām āmrādīnāṃ hṛdyānāṃ daśānām iti  eṣāṃ jīvanīyaprabhṛtīnāṃ phalānāṃ cūrṇitānāṃ militvā kuḍavo grāhyaḥ  anyad atirohitārtham  tathā hy ayaṃ prayogo jatūkarṇe ca paṭhyate drākṣākharjūramāṣājaḍāgodhūmaśālighṛtānāṃ kuḍavaḥ tilamudgau dvikauḍavikau cūrṇayitvā ityādi ghṛtaṃ śatāvarīgarbhaṃ kṣīre daśaguṇe pacet śarkarāpippalīkṣaudrayuktaṃ tadvṛṣyamuttamam  Caryurvedadīpikāghṛtaṃ śatāvarītyādau śarkarādīnāṃ prakṣepyāṇām anyatodṛṣṭanyāyād ghṛtāt pādikatvaṃ ghṛtasya prāsthikatvam  karṣaṃ madhukacūrṇasya ghṛtakṣaudrasamāṃśikam prayuṅkte yaḥ payaścānu nityavegaḥ sa nā bhavet  Caryurvedadīpikākarṣam ityādikāntāḥ pañcadaśa prayogāḥ  ghṛtakṣīrāśano nirbhīr nirvyādhir nityago yuvā saṃkalpapravaṇo nityaṃ naraḥ strīṣu vṛṣāyate  Carkṛtaikakṛtyāḥ siddhārthā ye cānyonyānuvartinaḥ kalāsu kuśalāstulyāḥ sattvena vayasā ca ye  Carkulamāhātmyadākṣiṇyaśīlaśaucasamanvitāḥ ye kāmanityā ye hṛṣṭā ye viśokā gatavyathāḥ  Carye tulyaśīlā ye bhaktā ye priyā ye priyaṃvadāḥ tair naraḥ saha visrabdhaḥ suvayasyair vṛṣāyate  Carabhyaṅgotsādanasnānagandhamālyavibhūṣaṇaiḥ gṛhaśayyāsanasukhair vāsobhirahataiḥ priyaiḥ  Carvihaṃgānāṃ rutairiṣṭaiḥ strīṇāṃ cābharaṇasvanaiḥ saṃvāhanair varastrīṇām iṣṭānāṃ ca vṛṣāyate  Caryurvedadīpikāghṛtakṣīrāśana ityādinā tu vṛṣyatvārthina āhārācārābhidhānam  nityamityanena vyavāyanityatayā śukramārgānavarodhena vyavāyaśaktiṃ darśayati  kṛtam ekaṃ kṛtyaṃ yaiste tathā etacca anyonyārtharāgakāraṇam  siddhārthā iti siddhasādhyāḥ akṛtārthā hi vyākulamanaso na kāmakṣamāḥ  vṛṣāyata iti upacitapravṛttyunmukhaśukro bhavati  mattadvirephācaritāḥ sapadmāḥ salilāśayāḥ jātyutpalasugandhīni śītagarbhagṛhāṇi ca  Carnadyaḥ phenottarīyāśca girayo nīlasānavaḥ unnatir nīlameghānāṃ ramyacandrodayā niśāḥ  Carvāyavaḥ sukhasaṃsparśāḥ kumudākaragandhinaḥ ratibhogakṣamā rātryaḥ saṃkocāguruvallabhāḥ  Caryurvedadīpikāmattadvirephācaritāḥ ityādi gṛhāṇi ca ityantaṃ yogyatayā ṛtuvibhāgenānuktam api grīṣmaeva jñeyaṃ meghānāṃ ityantaṃ prāvṛṣi tathā gandhina ityantaṃ śaradi vallabhā ityantaṃca vidhānaṃ hemantaśiśirayor jñeyam  saṃkocaṃ kuṅkumaṃ saṃkocāguruṇoḥ samālabhanārthaṃ vallabhā yāsu niśāsu tās tathā  sukhāḥ sahāyāḥ parapuṣṭaghuṣṭāḥ phullā vanāntā viśadānnapānāḥ gāndharvaśabdāśca sugandhayogāḥ sattvaṃ viśālaṃ nirupadravaṃ ca  Carsiddhārthatā cābhinavaśca kāmaḥ strī ātmajasyeti manmathasya  jātamadaḥ kālo vasantādiḥ   CarakasaṃhitāCikitsāsthāna Vājīkaraṇādhyāya Pumāñjātabalādikaathātaḥ pumāñjātabalādikaṃ vājīkaraṇapādaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ  Cariti ha smāha striyo vrajet yathā cāpatyavān sadyo bhavet tad upadekṣyate  Carna hi jātabalāḥ sarve narāś cāpatyabhāginaḥ bṛhaccharīrā balinaḥ santi nārīṣu durbalāḥ  Carsanti cālpāśrayāḥ strīṣu balavanto bahuprajāḥ prakṛtyā cābalāḥ santi santi cāmayadurbalāḥ  Carnarāścaṭakavat kecid vrajanti bahuśaḥ striyam gajavacca prasiñcanti kecin na bahugāminaḥ  Carkālayogabalāḥ kecit kecidabhyasanadhruvāḥ kecitprayatnairvyajyante vṛṣāḥ kecit svabhāvataḥ  Cartasmāt prayogānvakṣyāmo durbalānāṃ balapradān sukhopabhogān balināṃ bhūyaśca balavardhanān  Carpūrvaṃ śuddhaśarīrāṇāṃ nirūhaiḥ sānuvāsanaiḥ balāpekṣī prayuñjīta śukrāpatyavivardhanān  Carghṛtatailarasakṣīraśarkarāmadhusaṃyutāḥ vastayaḥ saṃvidhātavyāḥ kṣīramāṃsarasāśinām  Caryurvedadīpikājātabalatve saty api nāvaśyam apatyabhāgitvaṃ bhavatīti vā yathā jātabalaḥ ityuktepi yathā cāpatyavān bhavet yuktam  tadeva śukravaicitryaṃ sphoṭayati na hītyādi  na hi jātabalāḥ sarve ityekaḥ pakṣaḥ tathā narā nāpatyabhāginaḥ sarva iti dvitīyaḥ pakṣo jñeyaḥ  etacchukrabalabhedaprasaṅgād aparānapi śukrabalaviśeṣān āha bṛhaccharīrā ityādi  alpāśrayā alpaśarīrāḥ ete ca śukrasāratvena narīṣu balavanto bahuprajāśca bhavanti  gajavat prasiñcantīti śukraṃ bahu visṛjanti  kālayogena hemantādikālasambandhena vyavāye balavanto bhavantīti kālayogabalāḥ  abhyasanadhruvā iti vyavāyābhyāsenaiva vyavāyasamarthā bhavanti  evaṃ prayatnair vyajyanta iti vṛṣyaprayogaiḥ strīṣu pravartante  sukhopabhogān iti sukhānuṣṭhānān  nirūhānuvāsanaśuddhānāṃ vṛṣyaprayogāḥ phaladā bhavantīti nirūhānuvāsanābhidhānam  piṣṭvā varāhamāṃsāni dattvā maricasaindhave kolavadgulikāḥ kṛtvā tapte sarpiṣi vartayet  Carvartanastambhitāstāśca prakṣepyāḥ kaukkuṭe rase ghṛtāḍhye gandhapiśune dadhidāḍimasārike  Caryathā na bhindyād gulikās tathā taṃ sādhayed rasam taṃ piban bhakṣayaṃs tāśca labhate śukramakṣayam  Carmāṃsānām evam anyeṣāṃ medyānāṃ kārayedbhiṣak guṭikāḥ sarasās tāsāṃ prayogaḥ śukravardhanaḥ  Caryurvedadīpikāvartanastambhitā iti vartanena kaṭhinīkṛtāḥ  dadhidāḍimasārābhyāṃ saṃskṛtaṃ dadhidāḍimasārikam  dāḍimasāraśca dāḍimarasaḥ  māṃsānāmityādi atideśayogo dvitīyaḥ  medyānāmiti medurāṇām  māṣānaṅkuritāñchuddhān vituṣān sājaḍāphalān ghṛtāḍhye māhiṣarase dadhidāḍimasārike  Carprakṣipenmātrayā yukto dhānyajīrakanāgaraiḥ bhuktaḥ pītaśca sa rasaḥ kurute śukramakṣayam  Caryurvedadīpikāajaḍā śūkaśimbī  bhuktaḥ pītaśceti pūrvayogavad dhanabhāgasya bhojanaṃ dravasya ca pānaṃ jñeyam  ārdrāṇi matsyamāṃsāni śapharīrvā subharjitāḥ tapte sarpiṣi yaḥ khādetsa gacchet strīṣu na kṣayam  Carghṛtabhṛṣṭān rase chāge rohitān phalasārike anupītarasān snigdhānapatyārthī prayojayet  Caryurvedadīpikāmatsyaśabdena pradhānakalpanayā rohitaṃ vadanti  phalasārika iti dāḍimāmalakādiphalasārasaṃskṛtam  kuṭṭakaṃ matsyamāṃsānāṃ hiṅgusaindhavadhānyakaiḥ yuktaṃ godhūmacūrṇena ghṛte pūpalikāḥ pacet  Carmāhiṣe ca rase matsyān snigdhāmlalavaṇān pacet rase cānugate māṃsaṃ pothayettatra cāvapet  Carmaricaṃ jīrakaṃ dhānyamalpaṃ kuṭṭanenāṇuśaḥ kṛtam  māṣātmaguptāgodhūmaśāliṣaṣṭikapaiṣṭikam śarkarāyā vidāryāśca cūrṇamikṣurakasya ca  Carsaṃyojya masṛṇe kṣīre ghṛte pūpalikāḥ pacet payonupānāstāḥ śīghraṃ kurvanti vṛṣatāṃ parām  Carśarkarāyāstulaikā syādekā gavyasya sarpiṣaḥ prastho vidāryāścūrṇasya pippalyāḥ prastha eva ca  Carardhāḍhakaṃ tugākṣīryāḥ kṣaudrasyābhinavasya ca tatsarvaṃ mūrchitaṃ tiṣṭhen mārttike ghṛtabhājane  Carmātrāmagnisamāṃ tasya prātaḥ prātaḥ prayojayet eṣa vṛṣyaḥ paraṃ yogo balyo bṛṃhaṇa eva ca  Caryurvedadīpikāikṣurakaḥ kokilākṣaḥ  śatāvaryā vidāryāśca tathā māṣātmaguptayoḥ śvadaṃṣṭrāyāśca niṣkvāthāñjaleṣu ca pṛthak pṛthak  Carsādhayitvā ghṛtaprasthaṃ payasyaṣṭaguṇe punaḥ śarkarāmadhuyuktaṃ tadapatyārthī prayojayet  Caryurvedadīpikāśarkarāmadhusaṃyuktamityatra prakṣepanyāyāt pādikatvaṃ śarkarāmadhunoḥ  ghṛtapātraṃ śataguṇe vidārīsvarase pacet siddhaṃ punaḥ śataguṇe gavye payasi sādhayet  Carśarkarāyāstugākṣīryāḥ kṣaudrasyekṣurakasya ca pippalyāḥ sājaḍāyāśca bhāgaiḥ pādāṃśikairyutam  Carguṭikāḥ kārayedvaidyo yathā sthūlamudumbaram tāsāṃ prayogātpuruṣaḥ kuliṅga iva hṛṣyati  Caryurvedadīpikāpādāṃśikairiti ghṛtāpekṣayā pādapramāṇaiḥ  sitopalāpalaśataṃ tadardhaṃ navasarpiṣaḥ Caryurvedadīpikātṛṣṇāprāgrūpam āha prāgrūpam ityādi  prāgrūpakathane eva madhye tṛṣṇānāmavyabhicārilakṣaṇam āha svalakṣaṇam ityādi  svalakṣaṇam iti avyabhicārilakṣaṇaṃ yathā jvarasya saṃtāpaḥ
